<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Goal</h1><a id="user-content-goal" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Goal" href="#goal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The goal of this document is to provide the framework for OCP Specification contributions.</p>
<p dir="auto">This is a working version presenting an initial, evolving framework intended to establish alignment and guide future refinements.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scope</h1><a id="user-content-scope" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scope" href="#scope"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The framework will establish a common approach by aligning expectations, providing guidelines, and offering instructions for creating specification contributions.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Expectations: Define what is required from contributors to meet specification standards.</li>
<li>Guidelines: Outline the recommended structure and content for specifications.</li>
<li>Instructions: Detail how to use the provided template to create and submit your specification.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Specification Usage and Types</h1><a id="user-content-specification-usage-and-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Specification Usage and Types" href="#specification-usage-and-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The scope of contributions within OCP is broad, ranging from silicon to systems, and from individual systems to complete data centers.
To enable specifications across this wide span, we start with high-level constructs and incorporate significant flexibility to accommodate diverse needs.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usages</h2><a id="user-content-usages" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usages" href="#usages"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For any framework to succeed, it must be grounded in a clear understanding of use cases. To guide the framework definition, three primary usage categories are identified:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Introduce a new technology/direction to the community</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Rapid decision making enabling quick release of a contribution</li>
<li>Initial revision is typically sufficient for narrow, specific implementation</li>
<li>May require additional community work to address broader needs</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li>Enabling a full ecosystem</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Builds on an existing baseline (any source), to evolve or define a specification for the broader ecosystem</li>
<li>Expanded use cases and thorough vetting equates to a slower process</li>
<li>Typically has stepping-stone approach, adding use cases with each revision</li>
</ul>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>Technology development/evolution</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Planned technology development requiring strong community engagement</li>
<li>Planned progression through multiple revisions (0.3, 0.5, 0.8, 1.0) to achieve final, implementable results</li>
<li>Represents the slowest progression and highest detail level</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">These three usage categories apply across all levels, from architecture to implementation, and any contribution may align with each category throughout its revisions. When evaluating the framework, key considerations include:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Detail level: Comprehensive specification details vs. “Good enough” specification</li>
<li>Industry alignment: many specification are tightly aligned to industry standards and may need additional considerations</li>
<li>Flexibility for innovation: Allowance for exploration w/o having a predefined roadmap</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Types</h2><a id="user-content-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Types" href="#types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The three types or layers of OCP specifications are Base, Design, and Product.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/opencomputeproject/ocp-spec-template-process/blob/main/images/layers.png"><img src="/opencomputeproject/ocp-spec-template-process/raw/main/images/layers.png" alt="Responsive Image" style="height: 50%; max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Any or all of the layers could be utilized for any particular contribution.<br>
Examples:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A base layer defines the architecture and requirements for a nuclear power source for an AI Datacenter. The subsequent design specification details how to meet the base requirements with specific design elements and more detailed requirements for a Molten Salt Reactor (MSR). The final specification, the product spec, provides the implementation details (and potentially manufacturing files) for the "MSRv5 Power Module", a fifth generation MSR from the Nuclear Are Us store.</li>
<li>The Nuclear Are Us store provides (only) a design specification in order to create a larger supplier base for the MSR.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Base</h3><a id="user-content-base" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Base" href="#base"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The Base Specification is an architectural framework for coarse alignment providing requirements for flexible hardware and software modules/layers to interoperate. Market requirements drive Base Specifications. Without defining details of a specific design, the Base Specification may be light on IP content. This structure enables and simplifies the process for multiple parties (including potential competitors) to engage in this phase.</p>
<p dir="auto">This layer defines the technical details for one of the following:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Conceptual framework for an extensible technology platform/layer, representing technical community wide consensus and possibly used as a de-facto standard</li>
<li>Requirements for a specific solution</li>
<li>Extension/modification of an existing specification</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Design</h3><a id="user-content-design" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Design" href="#design"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The design layer goes deeper than the architectural specification by detailing how the system will be implemented at the component and module level.</p>
<p dir="auto">The Design Specifications has detail that further defines what specific role this contribution plays, and enough detailed design information such as high level board layouts etc that enables end users to begin the journey to realize this in the market. One or more parties may join to develop detailed design specs. Compared to the Base Specification, this effort typically contains significantly more detail such as IP-related information.</p>
<p dir="auto">Design Specifications are intended to foster multiple product specifications.</p>
<p dir="auto">This document defines the technical details for one of the following types of specifications:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Design Specification for an intended physical hardware product type</li>
<li>Modification of an existing specification (state which existing spec is being modified)</li>
<li>A specification with additional detail over the Base Specification for a product type.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Product</h3><a id="user-content-product" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Product" href="#product"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The product layer is an implementation-level specification providing the exacting details of the end-product.</p>
<p dir="auto">The Product Specification captures manufacturing requirements including all design and build files, building on the Design Specification.</p>
<p dir="auto">This document defines the technical details for one of the following types of specifications:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Product Specification for an intended physical hardware product type</li>
<li>Modification of an existing product specification</li>
<li>A detailed specification for a product type</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Guidelines</h1><a id="user-content-guidelines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Guidelines" href="#guidelines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">GitHub</h2><a id="user-content-github" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: GitHub" href="#github"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The following guidelines, together with applicable OCP IT policies, define the expectations for software contributions that incorporate GitHub‑sourced repositories.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Licensing Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-licensing-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Licensing Requirements" href="#licensing-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>All repositories incorporated into an OCP contribution <strong>SHALL</strong> use a license included in the OCP‑approved software licenses list (insert link to official list).
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Note that OCP specification follow the appropriate contribution license which may not align with the software license list.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Contributors <strong>SHALL NOT</strong> rely on repositories with ambiguous, proprietary, or incompatible licenses.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Preferred Repository Hosting</h3><a id="user-content-preferred-repository-hosting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Preferred Repository Hosting" href="#preferred-repository-hosting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>It is <strong>strongly preferred</strong> that contributors use repositories under the official <a href="https://github.com/opencomputeproject">OCP GitHub hierarchy</a>.</li>
<li>Use of non‑OCP GitHub repositories is acceptable when:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The repository uses an OCP‑approved license, and</li>
<li>The contributor evaluates long‑term maintenance, availability, and lifecycle risks.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>For long‑term viability, contributors <strong>should</strong> consider pulling non‑OCP sources into an appropriate OCP repository—especially when:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>it supports stability,</li>
<li>Customization or patches are anticipated, or</li>
<li>Dependency longevity is critical.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Specifications</h3><a id="user-content-specifications" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Specifications" href="#specifications"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Specifications have a defined process and associated templates. Any specifications hosted from repositories <strong>shall</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>align to/follow the appropriate specification template. This <strong>shall</strong> be measured via the PDF rendering submitted for the contribution</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Maintain version control per the specification process. The version <strong>shall</strong> use a tag for the specific version.</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Repository Documentation Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-repository-documentation-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Repository Documentation Requirements" href="#repository-documentation-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Every repository referenced within a contribution <strong>SHALL</strong> include a README.md containing at minimum:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Repository Description<br>
A clear statement of purpose and how the repository is used within the contribution.</li>
<li>Internal and external dependencies</li>
<li>Repository Hierarchy / Structure
Explanation of directory layout, modules, or tooling (if applicable).</li>
<li>Dependencies on OCP‑Approved Contributions
Include links to relevant OCP specifications or contribution database entries.</li>
<li>Contact Information (leads or support channels) as appropriate</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">No Guidelines</h3><a id="user-content-no-guidelines" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: No Guidelines" href="#no-guidelines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">No guidelines are provided for the following:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>workflow or branching model other than statements already made</li>
<li>repository structure</li>
<li>rate of development or maintenance</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Language Convention</h2><a id="user-content-language-convention" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Language Convention" href="#language-convention"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All specifications shall be written in English, and any recognized variant of English spelling (e.g., British, American, Canadian, Australian) is acceptable, provided usage is consistent within each document.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Modification of non-OCP industry standards</h2><a id="user-content-modification-of-non-ocp-industry-standards" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Modification of non-OCP industry standards" href="#modification-of-non-ocp-industry-standards"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">ToDo: complete this section</p>

<p dir="auto">question: Is there a better process to address OCP specification questions than an email to the project group.io?</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Normative Language</h2><a id="user-content-normative-language" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Normative Language" href="#normative-language"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Normative language establishes clear, enforceable requirements and removes ambiguity. Requirements are the basis for compliance.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Shall = requirement<br>
Requirements are mandatory, must be done.<br>
Including the word “not” (as in shall not) specifies a mandatory prohibition, meaning the requirement explicitly forbids the action.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Should = recommendation<br>
Recommendations are optional yet indicate a preferred direction if implemented<br>
Including the word “not” (as in should not) indicates a strong recommendation against performing an action</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">May = allowable<br>
Indicates flexibility of choice (option) with no implied preference.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Normative language shall be invariant to capitalization. This was chosen for simplicity as most authors do not rigorously follow the "all capitalized" standard. Authors following the invariant to capitalization guideline SHALL NOT use the keywords in their normal English meanings.</p>
<p dir="auto">The normative language above was selected for consistency and ease of implementation. This guidance is not intended to be restrictive. Conformance with the terminology defined in IETF RFCs 2119 and 8174 is acceptable. Regardless of capitalization choices, the selected convention must be documented in the "Conventions" section and applied uniformly throughout the document.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>All specifications shall utilize normative language.</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">References</h2><a id="user-content-references" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: References" href="#references"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>All references must be to published documents. Authors shall not reference documents that have not yet been published.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">For multiple related OCP specifications being developed simultaneously, cross-referencing is permitted provided that all referenced specifications have initiated the submission process to the Contribution Hub and will be submitted for approval no greater than three months apart.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is strongly preferred not to reference a document stored on an OCP Google Drive because such documents may be transient. Instead, the preferred approach is to release the document as an associated contribution and then use the Google Drive–hosted version only for “work in progress” material.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use of Non-OCP Document Information</h2><a id="user-content-use-of-non-ocp-document-information" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use of Non-OCP Document Information" href="#use-of-non-ocp-document-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>General Principle</strong><br>
All specifications must include only materials for which the organization holds the necessary usage rights or that are legally available for free and unrestricted use.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Best Practices</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Prefer Referencing Over Incorporation<br>
Whenever possible, reference external material rather than embedding it directly in the specification.</li>
<li>Avoid Version Lock-In<br>
Referencing helps prevent binding the specification to a specific version unless absolutely required.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>When Inclusion Is Necessary</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use Original Wording<br>
Describe the information in your own words whenever possible.</li>
<li>If Direct Inclusion Is Required<br>
Clearly state the source of the material.<br>
Ensure all legal and usage requirements are met (e.g., copyright notices, required attribution).</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Permitted Sources</strong><br>
Permitted sources would be those which allow legally free and unrestricted use.</p>
<p dir="auto">Examples of allowed sources include:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Apache</li>
<li>OIF</li>
<li>MIL-SPEC</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Vendor Information</h2><a id="user-content-vendor-information" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Vendor Information" href="#vendor-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Neutral Treatment of Vendors</strong><br>
Vendors must not be promoted or demoted in any documentation, communication, or system configuration.</li>
<li><strong>Component References</strong><br>
To the extent possible, avoid recommending components that can only be sourced from a single vendor. When a sole-sourced item is unavoidable, use neutral language such as “component XYZ or equivalent,” or consider defining a component specification that enables multiple vendors</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Versioning</h2><a id="user-content-versioning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Versioning" href="#versioning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Versioning shall follow the format: <strong>Major.minor.patch/errata (M.m.p)</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Increment Rules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Major: large functionality changes that may be incompatible with prior major version</li>
<li>minor: Adding functionality in a backward compatible manner</li>
<li>patch/errata: backward compatible corrections</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Currently, SW shall use the patch version. All other usages shall have errata = 0 until an errata process is established.</p>
<p dir="auto">Guidelines for usage:<br>
V0.3.0 = initial version with  sufficient content (e.g., TOC, vision, scope ...) to enable alignment<br>
V0.5.0 = majority of content defined; some areas need additional detail<br>
V0.8.0 = definition complete and implementable, though not fully reviewed<br>
V1.0.0 = reviewed and implementable across all capabilities<br>
V1.x.0 = use minor revisions for backward compatible changes.
V2.x.0 = use Major revisions for changes that may affect backward compatibility.</p>
<p dir="auto">Additional Notes</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Initial development is indicated Major = 0 (0.m.p) and any content may change at any time</li>
<li>Additional revisions between the designated milestones are allowed but generally discouraged</li>
<li>Versioning only increments; it never decrements</li>
<li>Versioning uses only non-negative integers</li>
<li>Regarding "complete and implementable", it is acceptable for a version to include elements intended for future definition, provided these elements do not hinder the implementation of the features and functionality defined within the current version</li>
<li>Any numbering statement in the specification name is part of the name, not the version (e.g. Recliner V1 V1.0.0, Recliner V2 V1.2.0)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Information outside of specification scope</h2><a id="user-content-information-outside-of-specification-scope" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Information outside of specification scope" href="#information-outside-of-specification-scope"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Maintaining consistency within specifications is critical to ensuring quality. Authors sometimes wish to include additional information that falls outside the approved specification template or does not align with its intended purpose.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>No content beyond the defined template structure shall be added.</strong>
The template provides flexibility for including supplementary details in the appendix section.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Review Guidelines and Checklist</h1><a id="user-content-project-review-guidelines-and-checklist" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Review Guidelines and Checklist" href="#project-review-guidelines-and-checklist"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Guidelines</h2><a id="user-content-guidelines-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Guidelines" href="#guidelines-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Define a minimal process &amp; checklist that each workstream executes prior to contribution hub submittal<br>
Checklist submitted with contribution</p>
<p dir="auto">Expectations</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Fully inclusive with defined minimum set of reviewers (content experts)</li>
<li>Invitations to dependent/adjacent workstreams</li>
<li>All feedback tracked &amp; dispositioned</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Final form verified to requirements before uploading to contribution hub</p>
<p dir="auto">ToDo: develop checklist</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">OCP Foundation Staff Review</h3><a id="user-content-ocp-foundation-staff-review" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: OCP Foundation Staff Review" href="#ocp-foundation-staff-review"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">OCP staff review specifications not only for alignment with the approved templates and guidelines but also for technical accuracy. Staff feedback is organized into the following categories:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Required<br>
Indicates feedback that must be addressed before the specification can advance to the next approval phase. This typically reflects non‑conformance to templates or guidelines, or a significant issue within the specification itself.</li>
<li>Recommended<br>
Indicates feedback that should be addressed to improve the overall quality, clarity, and usability of the specification.</li>
<li>Suggested<br>
Optional feedback intended to enhance clarity or usability, but not essential for approval.</li>
<li>Comment<br>
Captures all other observations, including occasional questions, often related to consistency or clarification needs. While questions are generally avoided at the staff‑review level, they may arise. Authors may determine if and how to address comments in this category.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Appendix - detailed Change list</h1><a id="user-content-appendix---detailed-change-list" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Appendix - detailed Change list" href="#appendix---detailed-change-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This section will be more a detailed direction enumeration than an explicit change list in order to help overall changes &amp; direction for feedback.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>2025/12/10</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Errata updates are suspended while we investigate usage (details available on the wiki).</li>
<li>publish a proposed base template which is a blank template with instructions as a separate document. The purpose is to ensure the template clearly displays the mandatory sections as well as shows the lack of mandate (flexibility) within the body.</li>
<li>Specification Guidelines serve as the framework for expectation alignment (i.e., mandates)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Normative language is required.</li>
<li>Revisioning is simplified.</li>
<li>The compliance section has been removed. This does not mean specifications will lack compliance requirements; rather, the format is under discussion. If requirement language is mandated, compliance becomes a summary of those requirements. (Status: WIP)</li>
<li>The requirement for product specifications to include design file contributions has been omitted. The community has not consistently followed this guidance, and its role needs to be reconsidered within the broader scope of contributions.</li>
<li>Additional guidance has been added for aspects such as vendor language and references.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>major items currently under investigation
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Compliance as noted above</li>
<li>Language for Base/Design/Product layers. Current wording in the guidelines originates from the 2022 definition effort. Since then, OCP’s scope has expanded significantly. The language and definitions are under review to ensure they align with and define the full scope of OCP, including considerations like design file inclusion.</li>
<li>Specification format. We aim to fully support a Markdown-based* workflow within OCP and encourage its use. However, it is unclear whether this will work for all specification contributions. We are investigating supported formats (Markdown, LaTeX, DOCX, PDF, etc.). *Note: Some contributors prefer Markdown with rendering flows, while others favor LaTeX. We are evaluating all options.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>2026/03/10</strong>
Compilation of the more significant additions/changes since last entry</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>added Foundation staff review information</li>
<li>Various clarification made in guideline</li>
<li>Various formatting changes</li>
<li>added GitHub Guidelines. misc formatting changes (ex. alpha order), reverted Citations to References</li>
<li>updated reference section with three month rule</li>
<li>updated component reference wording</li>
<li>added a Copyright/Trademark section</li>
<li>reverted Versioning to existing Major.minor.patch format with updated guidelines</li>
<li>added a detailed change list to guidelines</li>
</ul>
